< Review>
Great place to go car camping! Close to proximity to some wonderful hikes, and the bathroom situation is fairly better than most other campgrounds (though still not too great). Be warned though: the squirrels have associated humans with food, and will beg for food or rummage through your trash. Either leave your food in some solid storage like a cooler or hang it over a tree in a sack.< /Review>

< Text>
We visited this campground over last weekend Oct12/13. There is no option to book the campsite through online portals. All campsites are first come first serve basis. We reached the campground around 11.30a.m on Saturday morning. There were couple of unoccupied sites. One thing to note in these campsites is that the sites are not flat. So, checkout all sites for flatness to setup your tent before finalizing on one. The restrooms are equipped with paper towels, pit-hole toilets. The campsite is equipped with grill, fire-pit, picnic table, and water. One advantage with these campsites is that there is 11.5mi hiking trail just adjacent to it. We did hike a total of 4mi at our own pace. I plan to do 11.5mi hike in our next camping. We were not allowed to light the campfire in the night due to ‚Äúhigh fire alert - Santa Ana winds‚Äù. So, we spend time inside tent playing Uno. Overall, we had wonderful experience camping here.<//Text>

< Text>
Great first-come-first-serve camping site close to many good hikes. Keep in mind that there are not bear boxes available, even though the website says otherwise. There are also a lot of flies, and definitely no flush toilets. (They get pretty ripe when it's warm out.)</Text>

<Review>Our Experience at Manker Campground was overall good. We had grabbed a spot on a Thursday for the weekend because by friday there are no spots available it is a first come first serve basis. The 1st time we went we picked spot #8. We didn't like that spot much because we do have a little one & she likes to run around & the ground area wasn't that flat! The 2nd time we stayed we had stayed in spot #11 we thought this spot was going to be great they had plenty of trees to hang up our hammock but of course not great for our little one again & the neighbors that decided to stay next to us were up all night their music didn't shut off until 230am than they were howling like wolves like no one else was on the camp ground & than they had the nerve to project their Sexual relations very loudly & our daughter woke up & cried alittle than their sounds kept getting louder & louder. So our last spot was #14 we really enjoyed this spot it was a little more private we weren't in the middle of the campground. We were alittle more away from the bathrooms but thats ok. The only problem with #14 is that it has 2 sites to camp at like its for a group but only 1 parking spot!!! Luckily we arrived 1st than of course a HUGE!!!!!!! family decided to pick the spot next to us & the literally pitched their tent 5 feet away from ours like there wasn't any other spot to put it. So we kindly asked them to move it & they made a big deal out of it. But the overall experience was great I'm giving a 4star rating because of the fact that the bathrooms were smelly & dirty but what more can you expect being out in the wilderness at least there were bathrooms! Thank you Manker Campground for giving me a family a experience, we will of course continue to come here until we find the perfect spot were we aren't too close to neighbors. Pricing is really affordable! You can also day park here for $5 I believe.</Review>< Date>

<user_name>nethervortex<//user_name>< review>
Mon-Thurs and possibly Sunday night this place is a ghost town and a great place to camp at.

Fri and Sat people jam pack the campsites with 4+ cars at each site and party until 1am.  Which is great unless you wanna be up at 5am to go hiking.   With proper campsite selection you can arrive thursday and sell the large sites to other people to make your money back and then some.< /review>

< Text>
Small campground, clean bathrooms (for a campground) Went for 2 nights in July with my son and had a pleasant time. There are nice tall pine trees surrounding the camp which has nice picnic tables and fire rings. Great little get away camp less than an hour from Ontario.
There is a nice little hike near by, you can walk to the trail head, up to San Antonio Falls. There are a few longer hikes that you can do from Ice House Canyon trail head which is a short drive from camp.< /Text>

< time>
1536104347919<//time>
<Response>None< /Response></record>
</dataset><record>
<rate>2<//rate><time>1471765180128< /time>< text>
I love the whole Baldy area, including Manker Flats, which is why this campground gets 2 stars.  Beyond that, however...

When I arrived I began scoping out campsites, and immediately noticed that the whole area had been completely disrespected by previous guests.  Every site was littered with trash, and the one I would have chosen had a large, freshly-broken bottle right in the middle of the tent pad.  Most of the sites had at least a small amount of broken glass.  Also, almost all of the sites are right on top of each other.  At least most of the sites were fairly well shaded.

After finally selecting a site and starting to set up, I noticed the flies... LOTS of flies... So many buzzing around my head that I actually inhaled/swallowed one.  Ewww.  Now, I get it... it's nature... and late summer heat often means lots of flies, but it was still not a pleasant experience... and I have camped many places where I wasn't constantly under attack by flying insects.

Eventually, I needed to use the restroom... or not.  It was filthy, and the urinal was apparently clogged and overflowing.  I walked right out... a little ways away from the campground... and found a bush for some privacy.

I was sleeping in a hammock, so it wasn't until my friend arrived to set up his tent that I realized that the tent pads are a pretty awful dirt/rock combination that: make it hard to drive stakes; is bad for the bottom of tents; and can be rather uncomfortable to sleep on top of.

The grate on the firepit was almost impossible to manage.

The group with the campsite across from us was blasting music (electronic, hip hop, and either arabic or persian music) until at least 3 in the morning.

You are allowed 2 cars per site, but we really had to work to fit 2 cars into our parking space... Our bumpers were literally touching, and the front of his car was still slightly in the roadway.

We still had a great time... It's a beautiful place with some great hiking and fun stuff to do up at the Notch... but this campground needs work.< /text>

Unfortunately had a bad experience here and when we reached out to corporate nobody has responded so I feel I must share our experience publicly.

We ordered breakfast burritos and received the wrong  burrito. I tried to call back and could not get through, I ended up calling, and this is sadly not an exaggeration, eleven times before they picked up the phone. The person taking orders was Julius and he was not apologetic when they messed up my burrito the first time, he was even less so when we had to go back for the THIRD time because they had messed it up again. When I called (for the 12th time!) he actually chuckled and seemed to find it funny that the order had been messed up again. He blamed kitchen staff, however when I was there it appeared he continuously gave them the wrong order. They were the only ones who seemed to know what they were doing.

We tried to reach out to the Aztec Grill customer service email and have not received any type of response back. Unfortunately solely due to how Julius acted I can not recommend Aztec Grill to anyone, and we used to be frequent visitors.<//text>

< text>
This is my favorite local pho shop! I have been here probably 15+ times over the last 2 years and it never fails to disappoint. The large pho with beef is amazing, and they give you a good amount of meat plus a big bag of garnishes for takeout. No skimping on quality here! I usually order the crispy fried egg rolls with the lettuce wraps, and they are so good as well. I'll be eating at Vietnam's Pearl as long as I'm in the OC! Best cure for when you're feeling a little under the weather.

Ordering over the phone is easy, the lady owner is really nice and the food is always ready within 20 minutes. Can't be beat!<//text>

< Text>
The wait is always at least 25 minutes to get my order from the time I walk in to the restaurant to the time I begin eating. Today I had to wait 5 minutes to even be acknowledged as a customer. A party of 4 came in a couple of minutes after me and were greeted, seated, menus brought, and drinks ordered in less than a minute and ALL before I was even addressed. I always go alone and am casually dressed so I'm not sure if that has anything to do with the service I receive. I frequent this restaurant only because it's the healthiest choice literally around the corner from my work and I keep thinking/hoping the service will get better. Today it was the worst yet. I do have to say, however, that the woman (owner?) is quick, very efficient, and a good hostess. But she has been in the kitchen on all save for one of my visits. The food is good but it's your average Vietnamese dish at a south Orange County price. The vermicelli meat combo is $10, whereas, in Little Saigon 5 miles north I can get a greater quantity for $7 (same quality). If they had quicker service I'd give them 4 stars. Add on lower prices and it'd be a definite 5 stars. But, I get it, they have to pay rent and feed their families, too. FYI you can order food from their menu and eat it next door at the shakes place and vice versa since they share the same owner.</Text>

< review>
McCreery's is great and the furniture is very high quality.  We wound up there after declining to buy more particle board, I hesitate to even call it furniture, stuff from an office store.  The desk we bought will probably survive a nuclear blast but it cost a small fortune too.  On the other hand, the sofa and chair we bought are very reasonably priced and much better quality than the Recliner company recliners that I've had to reinforce a couple of times because they are stapled together.  The furniture McCreery's sells is actually good quality and well built.  My only complaint is their phone system sucks, it's terrible, I can barely understand them.

I had an issue with a desk chair (split in the leather seat) and they fixed it.  It took a little while for them to persuade the manufacturer to send the part but it came and they fixed it under warranty so I'm happy about that.<//review>

< Text>
The food, vibe and customer service was mediocre and I do not recommend.

I want to praise the great customer service and attention that server Alex gave us while there.
At the same time, I would like to condemn the actions and attitude of the server named Justin.

My boyfriend and I sat ourselves and the whole time we were there, Justin who was supposed to be the "assigned" server, NEVER checked on us, brought us anything, or took our order.

Instead, we were served and attended by Alex. While Alex was serving me, I hear Justin calling out to him in a condescending manner and ordering him around while Alex was busy attending other guests. This was very rude and disrespectful to do in front of customers.

The whole time we were there, I overheard Justin tell other guests multiple times how he was glad that he had a server to help (referring to Alex), as if Justin was Alex's master. Very rude and unprofessional.

At the end, I went up to the owner named Jose and explained to him the situation to which all I heard from him was a "thank you and sorry for the inconvenience". His response wasn't that of an understanding employer but more of an annoyed boss that isn't planning on taking actions to correct the situation.

Overall, this placed has a toxic work environment and I feel bad for the good workers that have to put up with it.

I gave this place a shot but will never be coming back and I hope it shuts down.< /Text>

< text>
The lunch atmosphere was pleasant and the ocean view patio made dining so much more relaxing. All of our food was very good, flavorful, and had a good presentation. The service was okay, could have been better. The lady at the dessert counter was NOT pleasant at all. She was short with me and I did not feel welcome at all, as I was trying to purchase an item like everyone else there. When I walked over to be with my party, she got in my face (assuming I was not with them) and said 'yeah...' I then simply stated, this is my husband ( a white man, and I am Black/multiracial) and though she might not have expected that, it was unprofessional for her to make assumptions because all people should be treated the same.

Our waiter was fine, but seemed overwhelmed and it took a long time to get the check. The lemons requested took a long time as well, but again the view made the time pass quicker so there were no complaints. I feel my rating is mostly effected by my initial experience with the lady working the pastries. I had a 10% Yelp discount, that they honored, but I went ahead and tipped on the higher amount. So the long and short--the food might be good but if people are treated poorly,for whatever the reason it may be, the entire experience is ruined.< /text>

<Date>1512917746731<//Date>< Rate>
4< /Rate>
<review>Streetside appeal beacons one come hither.
Entry dessert display and sales counter are the hook.
Decor, atmosphere, flow of table seating and bar area are the line leading you to the Oceanside deck where continued decor and atmosphere are the sinker.
I'm in!

Host, server, owner were all attentive and friendly.
Menu is extensive.
Quiche was to die for. Gorgeous. Flavorful. not America's typical shaken and stirred pie. This was layers of whole spinach, fresh sauteed mushrooms topped with gooey thickness of cheese resting in a no-crumb-left-behind pie crust.

Husband's burger on toasted brioche was perfection.

The dessert tray was successful at inviting to even the most full stomachs to eat just a little bit more our selections were tough, dry, weak flavor.

I liked C'est La Vie so much that I feel bad giving a review of less than 5 stars.
We vacationed in Laguna Beach. I feel familiarity with a restaurant and therefore, reviews need to be based on more than one meal.

Complimentary French bread before the meal was good, and they gave us more than enough for two.

We also ordered their chocolate bomb dessert to go- so good! Chocolate mouse filling inside a chocolate shell. The whipped cream on top was too hardened, so we ended up scraping it off. We would come back here again.< /Text>

while this place is not vegan, the chef will work with you to make your experience memorable. We came as a group and, given the French theme, I had little expectations for a vegan menu. < Text>
The view from the upstairs terrace here is magnificent. If you're looking for a nice place to have lunch and see the ocean on a pretty day, it's hard to beat. My seafood quiche wasn't quite as spectacular as the veiw. The crust was overcooked and tough, and the filling, although pretty good, wasn't particularly flavorful. The salad that came with it was very nice, but quite dry, to the point where I needed to request extra dressing. It's hard for me to say how much of this was due to the particular day that I went there vs how much is just the way the restaurant chefs prepare the food. I would definitely give this place another go!<//Text>

<text>Great LB experience. Food is excellent, drinks very good. Cozt patio with ocean view.< /text></record>
</dataset><record>
< text>
This place has a French themed but you can order from a variety on the menu. The atmosphere is comfortable and inviting to start; add Faredeh to the mix and you will feel right at home. This sort of personal involvement and care from the owner is rare in the restaurant experience these days! If you are a fan of French Bakeries, be prepared. you are greeted with some amazing pastries the moment you walk in. Just beyond that is the dining area with some great window seating for some world class people watching. There is a small and intimate bar reminiscent of an old world experience. If you are looking for a view, the deck overlooking the ocean is a highlight worth the trip in itself.  Wine selection is decent and their prices are very reasonable given the setting. This is a great place to start a day or wind down in the evening. The central location is perfect for either a beach day or a day exploring the shops and studios. TIP: There are a few parking spaces out back if you are fortunate enough to get one while it's empty< /text>

Since I live in the San Gabriel Valley, I usually go every few months or years.
The dishes that I have ordered have been good or excellent, 4 to 5 stars.  The service used to be very good, but now it is lacking.
That is why I rated it 3 stars.

I went on 11/10/18.  There is a sign which says to seat yourself.
I sat on the patio and picked up a menu that was already on the table.  Someone greeted me at the table and said that he would send a waiter. I was waiting for quite a while (didn't time it, but too long).  I noticed a couple arrived, sat down, and a waiter immediately went to their table and took their order.  He was tall, had an accent and was left-handed, which I noticed because I'm also a lefty.  I say this so that perhaps a manager reading this will identify him and speak to him in order to improve.
I almost walked out, but another waiter came to serve me.  Perhaps because I was alone, they thought I wasn't as important to serve.  A couple of years ago, I also received inferior service to those around me, I feel because I was alone.  This wasn't the case many years ago.

As far as the food, the Sea Bass with chipotle sauce that I had  was excellent.  However, to make the experience enjoyable, as it should be,
the service needs major improvement.
Other reviewers have stated this need just recently on Trip Advisor, etc.
The management should take note and make improvements.</text>< gmapID>

<rating>2</rating>< Text>
First impression was a very cute and aesthetically pleasing atmosphere. But the hostess and the busser were arguing about where my boyfriend and I should be seated. They were both telling us to sit at different tables.

The food wasn't absolutely terrible. I'm sure the crepes are good. But I didn't get a crepe. I ordered an omelette. It was supposed to be a southwestern-style spicy omelette, but what they brought me was the avocado and bacon omelette. Which I didn't really complain about because I was actually considering ordering that one, but it was very undercooked and watery inside. It was pretty gross. It was also confusing because two different people came to take our order at different times. The iced mocha was okay, but a little chalky.

What I did love was the violin guy walking around the dining room. He stopped at our table and played for a long time. Which was sweet and kinda romantic-y, but I guess we just weren't really sure how to act (should we just watch him play and smile, continue talking to each other, etc.) or if it was appropriate to tip him.

Overall it was a bit of a disappoinment and we felt a little like we had wasted our time and money üôÅ It probably could have been better, but that wasn't our experience.</Text>

< Text>
I really enjoyed my dish of the pasta mamma. I thought it was light yet hearty in a delicious, satisfying way. There wasn't too much Alfredo sauce, there was the perfect amount of eggs, bacon and the tomatoes on top sealed the deal. Absolutely delicious.

I tried the banana foster crepe which was sweet and satisfying as well. The view if you choose outside seating is gorgeous and I enjoyed eying their decor.

What brought down the rating for this place was the waiter. I'd hate to put so much emphasis on the staff, because we're there to eat. However, I feel that waiters/waitresses/ hostesses do make a difference. In this case, it was our waiter. The host who helped us to our table was very sweet and polite upon arriving and departing.

For starters, the waiter did not supply us with any bread. Everyone around us received it, except us until we asked for it. He took our order, then later returned with our food. Now we were celebrating my friends birthday, who specifically told us we had to try her sweet potato fries when they arrived. She told us before she even ordered it, as she was the only one who had been to this establishment before. The waiter then appeared with the food and asked if everything looked okay. The birthday girl mentioned she had ordered sweet potato fries, not the fries she was given. He immediately got defensive and said "you said steak fries." She said okay it's alright I will eat them. He then asked if she would like potato fries and she said no thank you. She was clearly upset. He said "are you sure?" as if he was annoyed. I jumped in and said yes, she would like her sweet potato fries.

This in my opinion was unacceptable. This could've been easily labeled as a miscommunication and resolved. First, apologize to the customer and then politely inform them you will correct the order and bring them out as soon as possible. It's really not that hard. He was just a bad waiter over all and really brought down the mood.<//Text>

<Rating>4<//Rating><review>The food at C'est La Vie was very special.. 5 star. I ordered simple, a Tuna Salad sandwich on rye and was I ever surprised. The sandwich was delicious, the bread was fantastic (light and great texture), then they served a pasta salad (which came with it). Best pasta salad I have ever had.

I met and congratulated the cook (Daniel), he happened to come out of the kitchen for a short time. Additionally, the waitstaff was great and the atmosphere is pleasant.

They also have a great patio overlooking Main Beach Park and the ocean. I love this place.

Note: I would give C'est La Vie a 5 star review  except the manager was very rude (before this writing I asked several people about the restaurant and the young manager (35 ish); every single one said he is rude), This manager certainly could work on his friendliness and be more professional with his customers. On the otherhand, the owner is an older man, he and his sister were very nice. Should be 5 Stars for sure!

<Name>Bev Graham< /Name><user>118039366177057698211<//user><rate>5<//rate><review>My friend and I tried C'est La Vie, yesterday for dinner, using a Travelzoo voucher.  We were not sure what to expect after reading the reviews.  We were very pleasantly surprised.  The manager was very attentive and made sure the server was told about us as soon as we sat down.  He came by several times during the meal to make sure everything was to our liking.

We sat on the covered part of the outside patio.  The forecast had been for rain, but the sun came out.  It was lovely and very comfortable.

Our server was very attentive to us as well as were all the other servers as they walked by---taking empty dishes and filling our water glasses, etc..

The food was delicious!  We had Jumbo Mushrooms with crab for an appetizer.  I had Sea Bass and he had Seafood Fettuccine for the main course.  My friend is from NYC and we have not found any restaurant in OC that he considers as having very good food.  This is the first restaurant that we have found  that he said has very good food!!!

The food is pricey as it is in most French restaurants. Because we were using a Travelzoo voucher, we were very pleased with our experience in every way!</review>< Pics>

< Text>
Come for the seating next to beach, but don't come for the food. Took my wife here for her birthday and we were expecting French cuisine. The menu is French enough having many of the traditional items. I ordered a Ahi Tartarte for appetizer and it was underwhelming both in looks and taste, not to mention the brown, spotted avocados.

For our entree, wife had the Canard A L'Orange and I had the Entrecote with the ubiquitous peppercorn creme sauce. The duck was soggy and overcooked, tasted like day(s) old food. My ribeye was a fat, sloppy cut, a bit undercooked, but the sauce was a sweet, tangy mess with no peppercorns anywhere. It felt like the chef cooks whatever/however he wanted and haven't read the menu. We were so disappointed with the food we didn't even finish it and decided to pay and leave.

The service was decent enough, but will not be coming back nor recommend any friends to come.</Text>

<Review>My wife and I ate dinner at C'est La Vie on Monday February 8, 2010.  The meal was excellent, reasonably priced and complimented by courteous staff and our waitress was extremely attentive and friendly.
